## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## DWS - Business Analyst (E-invoicing) - Requirements & Responsibilities (Translated to English)

Here's a breakdown of the requirements and responsibilities extracted from the job description, categorized as "Your Tasks" and "Your Profile."

## Your Tasks

*   **E-Invoicing Process:**
    *   Develop and implement e-invoicing processes, including standard implementation.
    *   Centralize global invoice verification processes.
*   **Invoice Data Integrity:**
    *   Verify invoice information, ensuring accuracy and compliance with legal frameworks and contracts.
    *   Monitor fee transactions to ensure timely and accurate payments and postings.
    *   Analyze and resolve invoice discrepancies (cash breaks).
*   **Data & Reporting:**
    *   Provide data to finance departments and generate reports.
*   **Stakeholder Management:**
    *   Collaborate with internal and external stakeholders (e.g., contract management, finance, custodians, customers, IT).
*   **Process Improvement:**
    *   Critically evaluate and understand new contract additions and system configurations from an operational perspective.
    *   Support the design and implementation of strategies to ensure continuous process improvement, define change projects, and improve service delivery.
    *   Document, standardize, and improve methods and processes.
*   **Strategic Execution:**
    *   Implement business strategies and goals across various product and business areas, adhering to internal and external regulations, KODs, SLAs, KPIs, and KRIs.
*   **Project Work:**
    *   Participate in project work.
*   **Compliance:**
    *   Ensure compliance with internal and external regulations, contracts, and policies.

## Your Profile

*   **Education & Experience:**
    *   Successfully completed studies in economics or comparable training.
    *   Experience in operations within asset management.
    *   Bookkeeping knowledge, preferably in fund or financial accounting.
*   **Technical Skills:**
    *   Proficiency in MS Office applications (especially Excel).
    *   (Advantageous) Product and system knowledge (SimCorp Dimension/Aladdin/SAP).
*   **Language Skills:**
    *   Excellent German and English (written and spoken).
    *   (Advantageous) French.
*   **Soft Skills & Personal Attributes:**
    *   Strong problem-solving and customer-oriented communication skills.
    *   High level of initiative and self-confident decision-making.
    *   Willingness to improve the status quo and achieve measurable results.
    *   Potential for further development and a high sense of responsibility.
    *   Teamwork and willingness to share information and expertise.
    *   Openness to new approaches and continuous learning.
*   **Other:**
    *   Experience in dealing with internal and external customers and service providers.
    *   Helpfulness and team spirit.
    *   Openness and ability to exchange information within the team.
    *   Commitment to supporting the company's CSR strategy (climate change, social justice).
    *   Interest in flexible and hybrid work arrangements.
    *   Adaptability to the company culture of responsibility, business acumen, initiative, and goal-oriented collaboration.
- **Validated Location**: Frankfurt

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Requirements for Information Security Specialist (m/f/d)

Here's a breakdown of the skills, experience, and knowledge required for this role, translated into English:

**Core Skills & Experience:**

*   **IT and Information Security Expertise:** Solid professional experience in IT security and information security, encompassing both technical and organizational aspects.
*   **Security Controls:** Knowledge of technical and organizational security controls.
*   **Communication:** Excellent communication skills in both German and English.
*   **Industry Knowledge:** Strong understanding of the banking and financial industry, including the impact of security risks.
*   **Standards & Frameworks:** Experience with ISO27001 and current industry-specific standards and frameworks (NIST, EISA, SOC2, PCI, MITRE ATT&CK).
*   **Cloud Security:** Familiarity with Cloud Security Alliance (CSA), Cloud Controls Matrix (CCM), and CSS Consensus Assessment Initiative Questionnaire (CAIQ).
*   **Regulations:** Knowledge of relevant financial regulations and guidelines (e.g., EU Cyber Security Regulation, MAS & HKMA TRM, EBA Guidelines, GDPR, NYDFS, SOX).
*   **GRC Tools:** Familiarity with Governance, Risk, and Control (GRC) tools, services, frameworks, and best practices.
*   **MS Office:** Very good knowledge of MS Office Suite (Word, Excel, PowerPoint).
*   **Assessment Programs:** Experience with Shared Assessment Programs (e.g., SIG, FSQS) is a plus.
*   **Data Reporting:** Experience with data reporting, including defining metrics and data sources is a plus.

**Responsibilities & Abilities:**

*   **Risk Assessment:** Conducting information security risk assessments with external partners (including on-site visits).
*   **Policy Review:** Reviewing information security guidelines and attestations of third parties.
*   **Analysis & Documentation:** Performing risk assessments and business impact analyses of identified vulnerabilities, and creating comprehensive documentation.
*   **Remediation:** Formulating measures to address vulnerabilities and close collaboration with third parties and project managers for problem-solving.
*   **Process Support:** Supporting and coordinating processes for reviewing information security at third parties.
*   **Monitoring:** Monitoring third parties and their security measures, escalating issues as needed.
*   **Contract Negotiation:** Negotiating contractual security agreements with third parties.
*   **Compliance Support:** Supporting compliance and risk assessment programs.
*   **Project Collaboration:** Participating in projects to improve the overall security control framework.
*   **Reporting:** Creating and presenting information security risks to various management levels.

**Additional Beneficial Skills:**

*   Experience with data reporting, including defining metrics and data sources.
- **Validated Location**: Frankfurt

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Requirements:

*   **Review Leadership:** Lead and conduct reviews of correspondent banking activities, focusing on client sectors and country-specific risks.
*   **Analysis & Assessment:** Perform initial analysis of clients and sectors, recommend clients for deeper review, and conduct comprehensive assessments of banks' Anti-Financial Crime (AFC) controls and governance.
*   **Risk-Based Analysis:** Conduct AFC risk-based transaction analysis reviews.
*   **Report Writing:** Author and own formal assessment reports.
*   **Advisory & Reporting:** Provide financial crime advisory based on review findings, present results to governance councils, and deliver regular reports to senior management on non-financial risks, control effectiveness, and compliance.
*   **Collaboration:** Collaborate with regional teams, internal and external networks, and lead site visits.
*   **Escalation & Updates:** Provide timely updates and escalate issues to the Global Head of CES.

## Profile Requirements:

*   **Experience:** Minimum 7 years of Financial Crime Compliance experience within a financial institution, with experience in correspondent banking and knowledge of local/international AFC and compliance regulations.
*   **Knowledge:** Strong understanding of AFC control and governance frameworks, including AML, KYC, and Sanctions policies/programs (e.g., transaction monitoring and sanctions screening systems).
*   **SWIFT & Payment Risks:** Strong knowledge of the SWIFT network and financial crime risks associated with correspondent bank payments.
*   **Teamwork & Stakeholder Management:** Experience working in a global team within a multinational organization, with proven experience engaging with senior stakeholders.
*   **Skills:** High level of initiative, strong work ethic, analytical skills, excellent attention to detail, and ability to work independently to meet deadlines.
*   **Language:** Fluent in spoken and written English.

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Audit Manager (d/m/w) - Requirements (Translated to English)

Here's a breakdown of the requirements for the Audit Manager position:

**Your Tasks**

*   **Coordination:** Proactively coordinate all aspects of the Endpoint Security Team.
*   **Deployment & Validation:** Lead and support end-to-end deployment processes and create high-quality validation of audit and regulatory activities.
*   **Team Support:** Assist in defining team responsibilities for each audit validation.
*   **Action Plan Review:** Review and provide expert opinions on customer-provided action plans, ensuring controls are effective and appropriately documented.
*   **Documentation:** Document workflows, progress tracking, process controls, and checklists to prevent recurring violations.
*   **Communication & Alignment:** Support and communicate audit plans and bank values within the team, ensuring understanding and alignment.
*   **Mentorship & Development:** Support an environment prioritizing talent management and development, demonstrating commitment to the team.
*   **Solution Coordination:** Coordinate and provide solutions in response to audit findings, working with engineers, architects, and business leaders.
*   **Risk & Compliance:** Contribute to an environment of technological solutions aligned with current regulations and guidelines, upholding the bank's audit and regulatory standards.
*   **Proactive Remediation:** Focus on timely resolution of open issues and implementing industry-leading standards for process controls and procedures.

**Your Profile**

*   **Education:** Bachelor's degree required; advanced degrees and relevant professional certifications preferred but not required.
*   **Knowledge:** Extensive and solid knowledge of risks, controls, and related regulatory developments.
*   **Experience:** Comprehensive audit experience within internal audit and/or the financial services industry.
*   **Skills:** Very good knowledge of management and planning, with the ability to drive positive change.
*   **Language:** Very good German and English skills (written and spoken).
*   **Personal Attributes:** Emotionally balanced, positive attitude, proactive, responsible, commercially minded, initiative-taking, goal-oriented, collaborative.
- **Validated Location**: Frankfurt

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Senior VMware Virtualization Engineer - Requirements

**Your Tasks:**

*   Develop virtualization solutions within a global internal private cloud environment using VMware Cloud Foundation (VCF 5.2).
*   Provision infrastructure platforms for virtual servers using automation (Infrastructure as Code - IaC).
*   Support global IT transformation projects by implementing requirements.
*   Translate business and security requirements into secure, scalable, and usable virtual solutions.
*   Develop new and extend existing architectures and automation processes within the VCF environment and related systems.
*   Analyze integrations with IT management systems (configuration, change, incident, security).
*   Manage complex global infrastructure processes to ensure stability and security.
*   Use Aria Automation and/or Orchestrator to configure virtual infrastructure environments and create development requests.
*   Contribute to Deutsche Bank AG's cloud strategy as part of a global team.
*   Strategically develop the VCF platform through design proposals.

**Your Profile:**

*   Bachelor's degree in Computer Science or equivalent experience.
*   Several years of professional experience in central computing and/or infrastructure virtualization (VMware virtual servers) in global companies.
*   Proven experience (several years) developing solutions with vSphere, ESXi, and VCF technologies.
*   Experience with common server operating systems (UNIX & Windows).
*   VMware vSphere and VCF certifications are desirable.
*   Experience with JIRA and GitHub is desirable.
*   Good communication and teamwork skills.
*   Fluent in English.
- **Validated Location**: Frankfurt

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Senior Tax Analyst - Requirements (English Translation)

Here's a breakdown of the requirements for a Senior Tax Analyst, translated into English:

**Your Tasks:**

*   **Tax Calculation:** Calculate current and deferred taxes for Deutsche Bank AG according to German commercial law (HGB) and IFRS, within the context of individual and group financial statements.
*   **Cross-Functional Collaboration:** Work with specialists and experts both domestically and internationally on various tax-related topics.
*   **Independent Tax Issue Handling:** Independently handle tax-related issues within Tax Reporting & Compliance, including documentation and implementing changes to tax laws.
*   **Tax Position Monitoring & Validation:** Ensure the monitoring and plausibility of tax positions for reporting units within the Tax Region Germany for the IFRS group financial statements.
*   **Process Automation & Standardization:** Contribute ideas and efforts to automate and standardize tax processes within the Tax Reporting & Compliance team, particularly within the GlobalTaxCenter and SmartTaxBalance.
*   **Tax Reporting & Compliance:** Responsible for fulfilling tax obligations, including preparing income tax returns and supporting tax audits.

**Your Profile:**

*   **Education:** Bachelor's degree in business administration or equivalent, with a focus on taxation, or a Diploma in Finance or equivalent qualification with current tax knowledge.
*   **Experience:** Several years of professional experience in Tax Reporting & Compliance within a group or an internationally oriented tax consulting firm, specifically in banking taxation.
*   **Technical Skills:**
    *   **Tax Law:** Solid knowledge of German tax legislation and experience applying tax regulations.
    *   **Accounting:** Solid knowledge of accounting standards (IFRS and HGB), particularly in deferred taxes.
    *   **Software:** Excellent MS Office skills (especially MS Excel) and SAP proficiency. Familiarity with GlobalTaxCenter and TaxBalance (Amana) or similar products is desirable.
*   **Soft Skills:**
    *   **Team Player:** Ability to work effectively as part of a team.
    *   **Proactive & Solution-Oriented:** Open to new content, responsible, independent, and solution-oriented work style, even under pressure.
    *   **Communication:** Very good German and English skills, both written and spoken.
- **Validated Location**: Frankfurt

**Your Tasks:**

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Requirements:

*   **Client Interaction & Analysis:**  Assist senior bankers in client meetings with C-suite executives to understand their business challenges and priorities, and identify potential mergers & acquisitions (M&A) and capital markets opportunities.
*   **Solution Development:** Create customized solutions for clients using technical, quantitative, and qualitative tools. This includes creating analyses, pitch decks, and project documentation for M&A and capital markets products.
*   **Product Integration:** Collaborate with product teams to develop product solutions focused on the bank's Corporate Finance offerings, and proactively integrate these offerings into client relationships.
*   **Client Relationship Management:**  Build and maintain professional relationships with key strategic clients (corporations, private equity firms, family offices) to establish trust and act as a reliable partner.
*   **Networking:** Build and expand a network within the technology/software sector and relevant stakeholders (e.g., private equity funds) to identify potential target clients.
*   **Project Management:** Lead projects as a project leader and experienced sector banker, acting as a key point of contact between product areas, industry groups, and regional teams.
*   **Reporting:** Report directly to the Head of the unit.

## Qualifications:

*   Bachelor's degree in Economics, Business Administration, Engineering, Law, or a related field, ideally with an international focus and a focus on Corporate Finance and/or M&A.
*   Significant, long-term experience in Corporate Finance, ideally with a focus on M&A, Equity, and/or Debt Capital Markets within a financial institution, corporation, or private equity company.
*   Experience and knowledge of the technology and software sector, including an existing network of contacts.
*   Experience working with project managers and company decision-makers, with strong communication skills at all levels.
*   Excellent project management and organizational skills, with the ability to prioritize and manage tasks under pressure.
*   Strong performance-oriented attitude, initiative, and willingness to travel.
*   Excellent German and English language skills, with strong presentation skills.
- **Validated Location**: Frankfurt

*   **Representation:** Represent the organization in internal and external sustainability committees and build relationships.

*   **Organizational Skills:** Ability to work effectively in complex organizations and deliver high-quality work under pressure.
*   **Interpersonal Skills:** Strong communication and networking skills, as well as diplomacy.
*   **Personal Attributes:**  Independent, detail-oriented, self-motivated, adaptable, and flexible.

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Senior Engineer - Requirements & Responsibilities (Translated to English)

Here's a breakdown of the requirements and responsibilities, organized into "Your Tasks" and "Your Profile" sections.

## Your Tasks

*   **Technical Expertise & Leadership:**
    *   Develop deep technical knowledge of Google Cloud Platform (GCP) applications.
    *   Lead and coordinate with regional and vendor Level 2 support teams (potentially across countries).
    *   Ensure application Service Level Agreements (SLAs) are met using monitoring tools.
    *   Provide technical support for routine (business-as-usual) applications.
    *   Perform post-mortem analysis and root cause analysis using ITIL standards.
    *   Improve service reliability by implementing SRE principles, proactive monitoring, automation, and operational efficiency.
    *   Mentor and guide junior team members, fostering technical development and knowledge sharing.
    *   Review production issues with cross-functional teams and drive updates/resolutions for outstanding tasks and recurring problems.
*   **Relationship Management & Collaboration:**
    *   Build and maintain effective relationships with stakeholders from business, technical, and vendor teams.
    *   Collaborate with stakeholders to deliver initiatives that improve stability.
    *   Proactively engage with stakeholders in critical situations.
*   **Process Improvement & Efficiency:**
    *   Proactively identify systemic errors and optimize manual/inefficient processes.
    *   Reduce recurring faults.
    *   Contribute to audits, maintain support documentation, and ensure compliance with regulatory requirements.
*   **Other:**
    *   Train and collaborate with junior support staff.
    *   Participate in audits.

## Your Profile

*   **Experience:**
    *   Prior experience as a team leader in practical IT application support.
    *   Experience in investment and transaction banking environments (a plus).
*   **Technical Skills:**
    *   Experience with cloud products, particularly Google Cloud Platform (GCP) and hybrid applications.
    *   Strong understanding of ITIL/SRE/DevOps best practices for production environments.
    *   Experience with monitoring tools (Elastic Search, Control-M, Grafana, Geneos, OpenShift, Prometheus, Google Cloud Monitoring, Airflow, Splunk) is advantageous.
    *   Proficiency in Red Hat Enterprise Linux (RHEL) ‚Äì log analysis, process management, command-line experience for troubleshooting.
    *   Shell scripting knowledge is a plus.
    *   Understanding of database concepts and experience with multi-relational database systems.
*   **Language Skills:**
    *   Fluent in English.
    *   German is a plus.
*   **Personal Attributes:**
    *   Proactive attitude, desire to identify root causes, and in-depth analysis skills.
    *   Strong communication and interpersonal skills.
    *   Ability to work effectively in a team environment.

- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Requirements & Responsibilities:

**Tasks:**

*   Design new network infrastructure and develop global standards.
*   Select network products to meet organizational requirements.
*   Gather requirements and determine solutions by working with stakeholders.
*   Conduct product testing and evaluation.
*   Present designs and standards to business leaders.
*   Train staff on specific technologies and designs.
*   Lead the design, development, and implementation of Zero Trust network solutions.
*   Develop, test, and document large-scale network solutions before implementation.
*   Lead Proof of Concept (POC) testing.
*   Create High-Level Design (HLD) and Low-Level Design (LLD) documentation.
*   Provide 3rd-level operational support.
*   Provide product training and support during handover to operations.

**Profile:**

*   **Education:** Degree in Computer Engineering, Business Information Science, or a related field.
*   **Experience:** Minimum of 10 years of professional experience in network security.
*   **Network Design & Architecture:** Solid experience in network design and architecture. TOGAF certification strongly preferred.
*   **Security Expertise:** Extensive design and engineering experience developing network security solutions for large enterprise environments. Industry-wide IT security certifications strongly preferred. IT Audit certifications are a plus.
*   **Technical Skills:** Deep technical knowledge of at least 2 of the following vendors/products:
    *   Cisco/Ariasta routing/switching
    *   Checkpoint/Fortinet firewalls
    *   Cisco ISE
    *   VMware NSX
*   **Skills:**
    *   Proven track record of designing large-scale network solutions.
    *   Strong communication and interpersonal skills.
    *   Ability to work effectively in an agile environment.
*   **Preferred:** Industry-wide certifications in IT security.
*   **Personal Attributes:**
    *   Positive attitude and ability to handle challenges.
    *   Commitment to continuous learning and professional development.
    *   Team player with strong collaboration skills.

*   **Teamwork:** Taking full responsibility for tasks within a small, focused team and collaborating with colleagues to achieve results.
*   **Communication:** Communicating complex topics clearly in both German and English, and presenting information in writing as needed.

*   **Knowledge:** A strong understanding of tax evasion prevention.
*   **Skills:** Ability to handle complex situations, work effectively in a matrix organization, and provide well-founded assessments.

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Requirements (Translated to English)

**Your Profile:**

* Bachelor's degree in Computer Science, Information Technology, Finance, or a related field.
* Minimum of 2 years of experience in SAP Software Logistics, SAP Basis, or SAP System Administration.
* Hands-on experience with SAP TMS, SUM, SolMan (ChaRM), and CTS+.
* Strong understanding of cloud-based SAP environments (SAP BTP, AWS, Azure, or GCP).
* Understanding of SAP HANA, SAP S/4HANA modules, and SAP Fiori applications.
* Familiarity with DevOps tools (Jenkins, Git, Ansible) for SAP automation is a plus.
* Strong problem-solving and analytical skills.
* Excellent communication skills for collaboration with IT teams.
* Fluency in English and German.

**Your Tasks:**

* Manage the SAP Transport Management System (TMS) to ensure secure and compliant movement of configurations and custom developments across SAP environments.
* Plan, implement, and manage SAP Software Logistics processes (e.g., Transport Management, Change & Release Management, CTS+ for non-ABAP).
* Optimize transport strategies and ensure compliance with best practices.
* Oversee SAP Solution Manager (SolMan) for system monitoring, change request management (ChaRM), and incident resolution.
* Integrate audit requirements & SDLC-process controls into SAP Development & Deployment workflows.
* Troubleshoot and resolve transport failures, deployment issues, system inconsistencies, and performance problems.
* Execute the strategy to modernize the SAP Software Development Lifecycle for all SAP applications in Deutsche Bank.
* Support SAP system installations and upgrades.
* Ensure compliance with financial industry regulations.

## Responsibilities:

* **SAP Transport Management:** Responsible for the secure and compliant movement of configurations and custom developments between SAP environments.
* **SAP Software Logistics Processes:** Planning, implementing, and managing processes such as transport management, change management, and release management.
* **SAP Solution Manager (SolMan):** Monitoring system health, managing change requests, and resolving incidents.
* **Compliance:** Ensuring adherence to financial industry regulations.
* **Strategy Execution:** Implementing the strategy to modernize the SAP Software Development Lifecycle.
* **Troubleshooting:** Identifying and resolving transport failures, deployment issues, system inconsistencies, and performance problems.
* **Collaboration:** Working with IT teams to ensure smooth and efficient SAP operations.
* **Optimization:** Continuously improving transport strategies and processes.
* **Integration:** Integrating audit requirements and SDLC process controls into development and deployment workflows.
- **Validated Location**: Frankfurt

Here's a breakdown of the requirements and responsibilities, organized into "Your Tasks" and "Your Profile" sections.

*   **Change Management:** Implements system changes.
*   **OS Security Compliance:** Manages OS security compliance.
*   **Incident & CIO Escalation:** Acts as a point of contact for critical incidents and CIO management, providing expert guidance.
*   **Cross-Functional Collaboration:** Serves as a liaison to other functional teams within Deutsche Bank (Storage, Databases, Engineering).
*   **Vendor & Service Provider Management:** Acts as a point of contact for UNIX vendors and IT service providers.
*   **Service Management:** Involved in service management for hardware and software matters.
*   **Team Collaboration:** Part of a team with internal and external members across three locations, responsible for OS support in the European region (EMEA).
*   **Expert Guidance:** Provides expert guidance to the team in UNIX and Linux environments.

**Your Profile**

*   **Education:** Bachelor's degree or equivalent in Informatics or a related field.
*   **Experience:** 10+ years of experience in UNIX system administration, including upgrades, patching, configuration management, performance management, capacity planning, and troubleshooting.
*   **Technical Skills:** Strong knowledge of UNIX-related technologies, including networking and storage.
*   **Preferred Skills:** Experience in UNIX operations within the financial sector.
*   **Optional Skills:** Bash, Python, or Perl scripting experience.
*   **Personal Attributes:** Strong problem-solving and analytical thinking skills.
*   **Language:** German language skills (optional).
*   **Teamwork:** Strong team player.

- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Senior UNIX Systems Analyst - Requirements & Responsibilities (English Translation)

Here's a breakdown of the requirements and responsibilities:

**Your Tasks:**

*   **Operational Support:** Responsible for all aspects of supporting UNIX servers within a global, 24/7 team.
*   **Workarounds & Bug Fixes:** Develops and implements temporary solutions (workarounds) and permanent fixes for system issues.
*   **Change Management:** Implements changes to systems.
*   **OS Security Compliance:** Manages and ensures compliance with operating system security standards.
*   **Incident & Management Liaison:**  Acts as a key contact for critical incidents and the CIO management, providing expert knowledge and support.
*   **Cross-Team Communication:**  Serves as a liaison to other teams within the bank, including Storage, Databases, and UNIX Engineering.
*   **Vendor & Service Provider Management:**  Communicates with UNIX vendors and IT service providers.
*   **Service Management:** Involved in managing hardware and software services.
*   **Expert Support:** Provides expert support within the EMEA region (Europe, Middle East, and Africa).
*   **Collaboration:** Works as part of a team with internal and external colleagues across multiple locations.

**Your Profile:**

*   **Education:** Bachelor's degree or equivalent in Computer Science or a related field.
*   **Experience:** 10+ years of experience in UNIX system administration, including upgrades, patching, configuration management, performance management, capacity planning, and troubleshooting.
*   **Technical Skills:**
    *   Strong knowledge of UNIX-related technologies, including networking and storage.
    *   (Optional) Experience with UNIX operations in the financial sector is a plus.
    *   (Optional) Experience with Bash, Python, or Perl scripting.
*   **Soft Skills:**
    *   Strong teamwork skills.
    *   Solution-oriented and analytical thinking.
*   **Language:** German language skills (optional).

- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Senior Network Engineer - Requirements & Responsibilities (Translated to English)

Here's a breakdown of the requirements and responsibilities:

## Your Tasks

*   **Network Architecture:** Design new network infrastructure and develop global standards.
*   **Product Selection:** Select network products that meet requirements.
*   **Stakeholder Collaboration:** Work closely with key stakeholders to gather requirements and determine solutions.
*   **Product Testing & Evaluation:** Conduct product testing and evaluation.
*   **Design & Standards Presentation:** Present designs and standards to business leaders.
*   **Training:** Train staff on specific technologies and designs.
*   **Network Solution Development:** Develop, test, and document large-scale network solutions before implementation.
*   **Network Security Expertise:** Focus on network security, particularly Zero Trust network architecture.
*   **Overlay & Underlay Network Design:** Design overlay and underlay networks.
*   **Software-Defined Networks:** Collaborate on designing software-defined networks.
*   **Proof of Concept (POC):** Conduct Proof of Concepts.
*   **Documentation:** Create High-Level Design (HLD) and Low-Level Design (LLD) documentation.
*   **Support:** Provide 3rd-level operational support.
*   **Product Training & Handover:** Provide product training and handover.

## Your Profile

**Education & Experience:**

*   Bachelor's degree in Computer Engineering, Business Information Science, or a related field.
*   Several years of professional experience in network security.
*   Solid experience in network design and architecture.
*   TOGAF certification is strongly preferred.
*   Proven track record designing large-scale network solutions.

**Technical Skills & Knowledge:**

*   Engineering-level knowledge of at least two of the following vendors/products:
    *   Cisco ACI
    *   Cisco EVPN
    *   VMware NSX
*   Experience with network security solutions for large enterprise environments.
*   Industry-wide certifications in IT security are a plus.

**Soft Skills & Attributes:**

*   Strong communication and collaboration skills.
*   Ability to work effectively with stakeholders at all levels.
*   Problem-solving and analytical skills.
*   Proactive and results-oriented.
*   Commitment to continuous learning and professional development.
*   Ability to thrive in an agile environment.

**Other:**

*   Fluency in English.
*   Openness to working in a global team.
*   Commitment to diversity, equity, and inclusion.

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Senior Operations Analyst - Tax Claim - Requirements & Responsibilities (English Translation)

Here's a breakdown of the requirements and responsibilities:

**Your Tasks:**

* **Tax Claim Coordination:** Coordinate and execute legal requirements related to double taxation agreements and the "FokusBank" legal case across multiple countries (Finland, France, Germany, Italy, Netherlands, Norway, Poland, Portugal, Spain, Sweden).
* **Stakeholder Communication:** Coordinate with local tax advisory firms and the Product Tax department to determine relevant investment funds.
* **Data Acquisition:** Ensure timely data acquisition involving internal and external stakeholders (front-office units, custodians, fund administrators, etc.).
* **Process Improvement:** Develop, implement, and continuously analyze processes to monitor and reduce operational risks and improve efficiency.
* **Issue Resolution:** Respond to internal (front/middle/back-office) and external (customers, regulators, tax authorities, etc.) inquiries regarding all Tax Claim processes.
* **Mentorship & Support:** Provide support and guidance to colleagues and functional teams to foster continuous improvement.
* **Project Management:** Initiate and coordinate projects to improve internal processes and performance efficiency and risk minimization.
* **Reporting:** Prepare requests from customers and internal (front-office) departments.
* **Process Oversight:** Ensure the timely submission of source tax credit and source tax refund applications.
* **Collaboration:** Work within a specialized team of experts in the international taxation of investment funds.
* **Problem Solving:** Develop and implement solutions independently.
* **Adaptability:** Work effectively in a rapidly evolving environment, proactively adapting to changes in tax and regulatory laws and embracing technological innovations.

**Your Profile:**

**Required Skills & Experience:**

* **Knowledge:** Understanding of the operational activities of an Investment Fund Company (KVG) and the relationships between involved business partners (investors, custodians, KVG, fund managers, brokers, etc.).
* **Technical Proficiency:** Routine use of MS Office (Excel, Word, PowerPoint, Outlook, OneDrive, Teams). VBA knowledge is a plus.
* **Tax Expertise:** Solid experience in the taxation of investment funds in an international context (desirable, but not required).
* **Organizational Skills:** Excellent self-motivation and organizational skills to ensure coordination of various stakeholders and timely processing of tax requirements.
* **Communication:** Excellent communication skills in German and English (negotiation-ready, written and verbal).
* **Stress Management:** Ability to maintain overview under high (time) pressure and deliver high-quality results.
* **Analytical Skills:** High aptitude for quickly grasping numerous and diverse tax requirements.
* **Problem-Solving:** Ability to develop and implement solutions independently.
* **Language:** Excellent knowledge of German and English (written and verbal).
* **Adaptability:** Ability to work in a rapidly changing environment, proactively adapting to evolving tax and regulatory laws and keeping up with technological innovations.
* **Teamwork:** Excellent teamwork skills, including openness and the ability to share information, expertise, and competence within the team.
* **Education:** Completed degree from an accredited university (preferably with a focus on tax or economics).
* **Experience:** Professional experience in tax advisory or auditing firms and/or in the operational tax area of a KVG is desirable.

**Personal Attributes:**

* Strong sense of responsibility.
* Proactive and results-oriented.
* Team player.
* Adaptable and resilient.
- **Validated Location**: Frankfurt

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Tax Senior Analyst - Requirements (English Translation)

Here's a breakdown of the requirements for the Tax Senior Analyst position:

**Your Tasks:**

*   **Policy & Guideline Development:** Help create guidelines and corporate standards, including documentation and analysis, especially for implementing global minimum taxation.
*   **Compliance Monitoring:** Ensure compliance with legal obligations related to global minimum taxation, both domestically and internationally.
*   **Analysis & Reporting:** Assist in creating analyses and reports for implementing global minimum taxation and its impact.
*   **Cross-Border Project Support:** Support tax projects that span multiple countries and collaborate with other departments within the bank.
*   **Cross-Functional Collaboration:** Work with specialists and experts, both domestically and internationally, on various tax-related topics.
*   **General Tax Support:** Handle general inquiries related to current and transaction-related corporate taxes.
*   **Pillar 2 Implementation:** Be responsible for the global implementation of Pillar 2, including developing guidelines for the entire group and determining tax bases to meet legal obligations.
*   **Tax Compliance & Reporting:** Implement Pillar 2 requirements and related tax compliance/reporting obligations.
*   **Consulting Support:** Assist the team with providing advice on various tax implications related to transactions or business events.
*   **Stakeholder Management:** Maintain close coordination with colleagues in the tax department (domestic and international) and local finance contacts in different countries.

**Your Profile:**

*   **Education:** Bachelor's degree in economics or equivalent, with a focus on taxation, or a Diploma-Finanzwirt or equivalent qualification.
*   **Experience:** Several years of professional experience in income or international taxation, ideally in a bank or financial institution, or an internationally oriented tax consulting firm.
*   **Certification:** Ideally, have successfully passed the tax advisor exam.
*   **Skills:**
    *   Excellent knowledge of MS Office (especially MS Excel).
    *   Proficiency in SAP, ideally with experience in GlobalTaxCenter and TaxBalance by Amana or a comparable product.
    *   Very good German and English language skills (written and spoken).
*   **Personal Attributes:**
    *   Team player with an open and eager-to-learn attitude.
    *   Demonstrates responsibility, self-reliance, and a solution-oriented approach, even under pressure.
*   **Additional Qualifications:**
    *   Knowledge of international tax law.
    *   Familiarity with tax regulations and compliance requirements.
- **Validated Location**: Frankfurt

- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Tax Specialist (d/m/w) - Requirements (English Translation)

Here's a breakdown of the requirements you need to meet:

**Your Tasks (What you'll be doing):**

*   **External Audit Support:** Respond to requests from external auditors during audits.
*   **Internal/External Liaison:**  Serve as a main contact person between internal and external teams within the Tax department.

*   **Audit Findings Review:** Review and evaluate findings from external audits.
*   **Inquiry Handling:** Prepare justifications for inquiries and conduct legal research and analysis for inquiry proceedings.
*   **Litigation Support:** Work with the team leader and external legal advisors on legal documents in litigation cases.
*   **Team Collaboration:** Communicate consistently with colleagues, team leaders, and other departments.

**Your Profile (What you need to have):**

*   **Education:** Bachelor's degree in Economics or Law with a focus on Taxation, *or* a Diplom-Finanzwirt degree or equivalent with a focus on German tax law.
*   **Experience:**  Must have passed the Tax Advisor Examination and have several years of professional experience in a corporate setting, international tax consulting firm, or law firm.
*   **Skills:**
    *   Strong communication skills and the ability to work effectively in a team.
    *   Demonstrated responsibility, self-motivation, and a solution-oriented work style, even when under pressure.
    *   Excellent written and verbal German and English language skills.

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Requirements (Translated into English)

**Your Profile:**

*   Successfully completed university degree in economics, real estate economics, or a related field, preferably with additional real estate qualifications (e.g., Master of Real Estate, Real Estate Economist, RICS).
*   Several years of professional experience in the comprehensive management of properties and/or relevant real estate internships.
*   Commercial understanding and secure handling of cash flow models.
*   Leadership experience managing a team.
*   Creativity, independent work style, and a strong commitment to tasks.
*   Persuasive presence combined with strong communication and analytical skills.
*   Fluent German and very good English skills, both spoken and written.
*   Solid experience managing properties with retail use or shopping centers; experience with healthcare and residential properties is desirable.

**Your Tasks:**

*   Lead a team of 5 asset managers.
*   Manage a portfolio of national commercial properties, with a focus on retail and shopping centers, owned by DWS open real estate funds and special funds.
*   Implement DWS Real Estate's sustainability goals within the assigned portfolio, including ESG measures, potentially in cooperation with external partners.
*   Be responsible for the performance of your assets, particularly identifying development potential and implementing it ‚Äì including managing restructurings.
*   Identify and consider trends and market developments in the strategic direction of real estate investments.
*   Select, award, and actively manage external service providers (especially center managers, leasing managers, commercial and technical property managers, technical advisors, architects, engineers, legal, and tax advisors).
*   Optimize real estate and financial aspects of the assigned properties, as well as revenue and economic calculations (e.g., using DCF analyses).
*   Create budgets and business plans, as well as hold-sell analyses, including regular quarterly reporting to Funds Management, and continuously identify cost drivers and revenue-reducing factors.
*   Act as a building owner in expansion and renovation measures and project developments, as well as support transaction management in sales and purchases.

## Responsibilities

*   **Team Leadership:** Leading and developing a team of 5 asset managers.
*   **Portfolio Management:** Managing a portfolio of commercial and residential properties with a volume of approximately 7.4 billion euros.
*   **Sustainability & ESG:** Implementing sustainability goals and ESG measures within the assigned portfolio.
*   **Performance Management:** Taking responsibility for asset performance, identifying development potential, and implementing necessary changes.
*   **External Stakeholder Management:** Selecting, awarding, and controlling external service providers.
*   **Financial Optimization:** Optimizing real estate and financial aspects of properties, including revenue and economic calculations.
*   **Reporting & Analysis:** Preparing budgets, business plans, hold-sell analyses, and quarterly reports.
*   **Project Management:** Acting as a building owner in expansion and renovation measures and supporting transaction management.
*   **Strategic Input:** Identifying and considering trends and market developments in real estate investments.
*   **Negotiation:** Negotiating deals and contracts with external partners.
*   **Mentorship:** Providing guidance and support to team members.
- **Validated Location**: Frankfurt

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## DWS - Know Your Client (KYC) Analyst (m/f/d) - Requirements & Responsibilities (English Translation)

Here's a breakdown of the requirements and responsibilities, translated into English:

## Your Tasks

*   **KYC/Sanctions Checks:** Independently conduct and document complete and timely KYC/Sanctions checks on new and existing national and international clients, considering global/local guidelines and relevant local regulatory requirements.
*   **Client Coverage Support:** Serve as the primary point of contact for the Client Coverage Division regarding KYC/Sanctions checks.
*   **DD Monitoring & AFC Collaboration:** Contribute to the processing of requests from CDD Monitoring and Anti-Financial Crime (AFC) areas.
*   **Process Optimization:** Participate in optimizing existing processes for efficiency improvements and simplification.
*   **Project Support:** Support and take over regular and ad-hoc special projects.
*   **Regulatory Compliance:** Implement new (process) requirements and support measures to ensure quality assurance.
*   **Management Reporting:** Assist the team leader in creating management reports.
*   **Collaboration:** Work closely with various stakeholders, including Client Coverage (CCD), Anti-Financial Crime (AFC), and Legal Documentation Management (LDM).
*   **Timelines:** Ensure all deadlines are met.
*   **Quality Assurance:** Contribute to maintaining high KYC quality standards.
*   **Network Building:** Build an internal network and contribute to maintaining high KYC quality standards.

## Your Profile

**Education & Experience:**

*   Completed university degree or vocational training (e.g., Bankbetriebswirt, MBA, CFA). Alternatively, completed vocational training with relevant further education.
*   Several years of practical experience in the finance industry in the KYC or Anti-Financial Crime area.
*   Solid experience in KYC with corresponding knowledge of legal requirements and guidelines, as well as the competence to implement regulatory requirements.

**Skills & Abilities:**

*   Ability to recognize and understand complex processes.
*   Strong communication skills, confident demeanor, reliability, and flexibility.
*   Ability to work independently, conscientiously, accurately, and reliably.
*   Enjoys working in a dynamic, international team.
*   Proficient in modern IT and fluent in German and English (written and spoken).

**Personal Attributes:**

*   Driven and ambitious.
*   Values a positive and supportive work environment.
*   Commitment to the company's CSR strategy (climate change, social justice).
*   Open to flexible and hybrid work arrangements.
*   Willingness to adapt to changing work environments and methods.
*   Commitment to responsible, business-minded, proactive, and goal-oriented teamwork.
*   Positive attitude and willingness to celebrate the successes of colleagues.
*   Commitment to a positive, fair, and inclusive work environment.

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Requirements (Translated into English)

**Your Background:**

*   **Education:** Bachelor's degree, preferably in Computer Science, Engineering, Information Technology, or a related field.
*   **Experience:** Significant experience in cybersecurity.
*   **Knowledge:** Strong understanding of cybersecurity capabilities, including designing and deploying security solutions.
*   **Certifications:** Cybersecurity certifications are a plus (e.g., CISSP, Security+, SABSA).
*   **Skills:** Excellent communication and presentation skills.
*   **Problem-Solving:** Proven ability to understand complex problems and create actionable plans.
*   **Familiarity:** Experience working in a large, complex organization.

**Your Responsibilities:**

*   **Strategy Development:** Help design and implement a security strategy for network security, aligned with organizational goals.
*   **Roadmap Creation:** Develop short-term and long-term plans for security capabilities within network security, keeping up with market and industry trends.
*   **Stakeholder Management:** Communicate with internal and external stakeholders to discuss dependencies, review architecture and technology, and ensure alignment across different teams.
*   **Cross-Team Collaboration:** Work closely with other security architects to maintain consistency in developing and delivering network security strategies.
*   **Strategy Advocacy:** Understand, promote, and support the company's IT security strategy, and improve the Security Pillar Domain Architecture program.
*   **Threat Analysis & Improvement:** Analyze the current IT security environment related to network security to identify vulnerabilities and recommend improvements, using knowledge of current threats.
*   **Technology Optimization:** Identify opportunities to improve the technology used in network security.
*   **Domain Ownership:** Be the expert and lead for the "Network Security" domain.
*   **Roadmap Development (Specific):** Create short, medium, and long-term plans for all security capabilities within network security.
*   **Dependency Management:** Manage dependencies for the network security domain with stakeholders across the organization.

## Responsibilities (Translated into English)

*   **Strategic Leadership:** Lead the development and direction of the network security strategy.
*   **Roadmap Planning:** Responsible for creating and maintaining short, medium, and long-term plans for network security capabilities.
*   **Stakeholder Engagement:** Manage relationships and communication with stakeholders across the organization regarding network security.
*   **Architectural Consistency:** Ensure consistency in the development and implementation of network security strategies within the domain.
*   **Strategy Implementation:** Understand, promote, and support the company's IT security strategy within the network security domain.
*   **Risk & Improvement:** Analyze the current IT security environment and recommend solutions for improvement within the network security domain.
*   **Technology Optimization:** Identify and propose opportunities to improve the technology used in network security.
*   **Domain Expertise:** Maintain and expand expertise within the network security domain.

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Requirements (Translated to English)

**Your Profile:**

*   **Education:** Completed university degree or comparable qualification, ideally with a focus on international tax law.
*   **Certification:** Completion of a tax advisor examination is an advantage.
*   **Experience:** Several years of professional experience in (tax) transfer pricing, particularly within the financial sector of an internationally active company or a large international tax consulting firm.
*   **Asset Management Experience:** Practical experience in documentation projects and the development and implementation of transfer pricing concepts in asset management or banking.
*   **Industry Knowledge:** Good understanding of asset management business.
*   **Skills:**
    *   Excellent ability to work in a team.
    *   Very good communication and expression skills, and a proactive, independent work style.
    *   Excellent analytical skills to quickly grasp complex issues and processes.
    *   Fluent in German and English (written and spoken).
    *   Excellent MS Office skills.

**Requirements:**

*   Completed university degree or comparable qualification, ideally with a focus on international tax law.
*   Completion of a tax advisor examination is an advantage.
*   Several years of professional experience in (tax) transfer pricing, particularly within the financial sector of an internationally active company or a large international tax consulting firm.
*   Practical experience in documentation projects and the development and implementation of transfer pricing concepts in asset management or banking.

## Responsibilities (Translated to English)

**Your Tasks:**

*   Contribute to the global transfer pricing concepts of the DWS Group.
*   Support the development of transfer pricing guidelines to adapt to legal changes and changes in business processes.
*   Collaborate with other teams within the DWS Group to ensure the timely availability of valuable end-to-end transfer pricing documentation to support the choice and application of the respective TP methods.
*   Close collaboration with the central TP Governance Team to ensure a robust process for creating valuable local files based on OECD requirements and continuous monitoring of implementation.
*   Together with DWS Group Tax, defend transfer prices in audits, particularly answering audit requests on transfer pricing topics in Germany.
*   Support DWS Group Tax in tax disputes on transfer pricing topics.
*   Establish transfer pricing methods and calculation rules in coordination with DWS Group Tax to ensure that cross-border performance relationships comply with OECD requirements.
*   Participate in the implementation of legal changes in the field of transfer pricing in Germany.
*   Serve as a Schnittstellenfunktion (interface function) ensuring internal consistency and coordination with Finance Directors (FD) and COO teams.
*   Support management of relationships with tax authorities in Germany in close coordination with DWS Group Tax, including during tax audits and in the event of tax disputes on transfer pricing.
*   Ensure compliance with essential guidelines and applicable tax regulations for inter-company transactions of DWS.
*   Advise on applicable TP methods and allocation keys.
*   Establish minimum requirements for transfer pricing documentation in accordance with OECD guidelines and define control points around the TP lifecycle.
*   Establish a governance structure to ensure compliance with these minimum documentation and control standards.

**Responsibilities:**

*   Contribute to the global transfer pricing concepts of the DWS Group.
*   Support the development of transfer pricing guidelines to adapt to legal changes and changes in business processes.
*   Collaborate with other teams within the DWS Group to ensure the timely availability of valuable end-to-end transfer pricing documentation to support the choice and application of the respective TP methods.

*   **Process Improvement & Digitalization:** Participate in projects focused on designing and adapting business processes to meet indirect tax requirements, and on further developing the digitalization of indirect tax functions.
*   **ERP Process Definition & Oversight:** Define and develop indirect tax processes within the ERP system.
*   **Compliance & Documentation:** Monitor indirect tax compliance and ensure ongoing documentation of used IT applications.
*   **IT Implementation Support:** Provide support for IT implementations related to indirect tax.

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## DWSH Legal Counsel / Senior Legal Counsel - Requirements (Translated into English)

Here's a breakdown of the requirements for the DWSH Legal Counsel / Senior Legal Counsel position:

**Your Tasks:**

*   **Contract Negotiation & Drafting:**  Advise on and negotiate commercial and cooperation agreements for investment funds and other financial products, as well as other commercial agreements, in both German and English.
*   **Contract Templates & Standard Documentation:** Develop contract templates, standard terms and conditions, and standard commercial customer documentation in both German and English.
*   **Regulatory & Strategic Project Support:** Assist with regulatory and strategic projects at DWSH.
*   **Legal Advice (Investment, Securities, Capital Markets):** Provide legal advice on all commercial matters related to DWSH's German entities, particularly in the areas of investment, securities trading, and capital markets law.
*   **Dispute Resolution & External Counsel:** Advise on legal disputes and administrative proceedings, and select and manage external legal counsel.
*   **Cross-functional Collaboration:** Work with various departments within DWSH to provide legal support.
*   **CSR Support:** Contribute to DWSH's Corporate Social Responsibility (CSR) strategy by supporting partner organizations or participating in corporate volunteering activities.

**Your Profile:**

*   **Education & Experience:**
    *   A fully qualified lawyer (with a First Class Diploma/Excellent academic record) is highly preferred.
    *   Minimum of 2 years of professional experience in investment, securities trading, and capital markets law.
    *   Experience in a commercial company or law firm is desirable.
*   **Language Skills:**
    *   Excellent German and English language skills (written and spoken).
*   **Skills & Abilities:**
    *   Negotiation skills.
    *   Strong analytical skills combined with creative problem-solving abilities.
    *   Interest and understanding of economic issues.
    *   Meticulous, structured, and independent working style.
    *   Affinity and enthusiasm for Legal Tech.
    *   Excellent teamwork and communication skills.
*   **Personal Attributes:**
    *   Enjoy challenging tasks in an international environment.
    *   Proactive and results-oriented.
    *   Values-driven and committed to work-life balance.
*   **Other:**
    *   Openness to flexible and hybrid work arrangements.
    *   Willingness to participate in DWSH's CSR initiatives.
- **Validated Location**: Frankfurt

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Compliance Testing Officer - Requirements (English Translation)

Here's a breakdown of the requirements for the Compliance Testing Officer position:

**Your Tasks:**

*   Identify and evaluate existing first-level controls within the Corporate Bank (CB), Investment Bank (IB), and Capital Release Unit (CRU) divisions.
*   Contribute to the development of risk-based testing methods and plans for the assigned area.
*   Plan and execute various testing formats (reviews, tests, adherence checks, and on-site audits) in compliance with internal methods and procedures, and participate in reporting.
*   Discuss findings and necessary actions with stakeholders, including senior management.
*   Support the implementation of agreed-upon measures and escalate overdue findings.
*   Participate in the preparation and execution of projects and initiatives related to new regulatory requirements.
*   Participate in international divisional Global Practice Groups.

**Your Profile:**

*   First professional experience in Compliance, Legal, Financial Audit, Revision/Audit, Divisional Control Offices/Business Control Units, Business Management, or Risk Management.
*   Specific experience in the conceptual development of methods and controls (WpHG, MaComp, and MaRisk) is highly desirable.
*   Knowledge of relevant regulations and the business environment, with a willingness to continuously learn new regulatory requirements, especially for CB, IB, and CRU divisions.
*   Analytical skills and a quick understanding to quickly grasp complex matters and processes, identify key risk aspects, and draw appropriate conclusions.
*   Strong communication skills, proactive conflict and escalation management, and goal-oriented, persuasive conversation skills.
*   Excellent communication and expression skills in both German and English (written and verbal).
*   Team player with high self-motivation and the ability to handle multiple tasks simultaneously under pressure, while meeting deadlines.



**Key Skills & Experience to Bring:**

*   **Compliance/Risk Management Background:** Prior experience in a related field (Compliance, Audit, Risk Management, etc.).
*   **Regulatory Knowledge:** Familiarity with German financial regulations (WpHG, MaComp, MaRisk) is a plus.
*   **Analytical Abilities:** Strong analytical skills to understand complex processes and identify risks.
*   **Communication Skills:** Excellent written and verbal communication skills in both German and English.
*   **Project Management:** Ability to participate in and contribute to projects related to regulatory changes.
*   **Adaptability:** Ability to learn and adapt to new regulations and requirements.
*   **Teamwork:** Ability to work effectively in a team environment.
*   **Time Management:** Ability to manage multiple tasks and meet deadlines.
- **Validated Location**: Frankfurt

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Regulatory Control Senior Advisor - Requirements & Responsibilities

Here's a breakdown of the requirements and responsibilities:

**Your Tasks:**

*   **Data Quality Management:**
    *   Understand and address AFC TM data requirements, ensuring data quality from relevant sources.
    *   Utilize Data Governance Framework, data processes, and tools (DQ Direct, Collibra, Waltz, Solidatus) to ensure compliance with guidelines and regulations.
    *   Drive root cause analysis for data quality issues, collaborating with data producers and IT to improve data quality.
    *   Collaborate with process owners to assess data control effectiveness based on key data quality dimensions (accuracy, completeness, timeliness).
    *   Create KPIs aligned with central metrics and methods.
    *   Collaborate with stakeholders across the organization (regional/global groups, AFC, DDO, IT, data producers) to ensure data quality.
    *   Manage DQ assessments against requirements for Transaction Monitoring (TM) modeling teams globally.
    *   Support the delivery of new/updated Data Quality rules & product refinements.
    *   Establish data quality requirements linked to business outcomes, using data lineage (Waltz, Solidatus) and metadata tools (Collibra).
    *   Implement and adhere to data quality standards and procedures.
*   **Analysis & Reporting:**
    *   Perform root cause analysis of data quality issues.
    *   Analyze data sets and present results to senior stakeholders.
*   **Collaboration & Communication:**
    *   Work with process owners, the CAO Data Office, business SMEs, program change teams, and technology colleagues.
    *   Communicate effectively (written and verbal) with stakeholders at all levels.
    *   Build relationships with stakeholders from various business, IT, audit, AFC & Compliance areas.
*   **Data Governance & Improvement:**
    *   Contribute to the development of Data Quality Management capabilities.
    *   Support the TM Data Steward Office in addressing regulatory commitments.

**Your Profile:**

*   **Education & Experience:**
    *   University degree or equivalent professional experience in Financial Services, specifically Anti-Financial Crime and Transaction Monitoring.
    *   Experience in Transaction Monitoring/Data Governance with a strong quantitative background.
    *   Experience in data analysis and root cause analysis.
    *   Experience in Data Governance and Data Quality Management.
*   **Skills & Competencies:**
    *   Excellent organizational and data analytical skills with attention to detail.
    *   Proficiency in Microsoft Office programs (Excel, Word, PowerPoint, Access), SharePoint, and SQL.
    *   Strong communication skills in English (written and verbal).
    *   Ability to work independently and as part of a team.
    *   Ability to build relationships with stakeholders from diverse backgrounds.
    *   Understanding of Data Governance, Quality Management, Modeling, and Analytics.
    *   Experience working on data projects across various technologies and data formats.
*   **Personal Attributes:**
    *   Emotionally balanced and resilient.
    *   Physically fit and health-conscious.
    *   Socially connected and collaborative.
    *   Financially secure and forward-thinking.
    *   Driven, self-motivated, and results-oriented.
- **Validated Location**: Frankfurt

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## IFRS Reporting Manager - Requirements & Responsibilities (English Translation)

Here's a breakdown of the requirements and responsibilities:

**Your Tasks**

*   **Financial Reporting:**
    *   Prepare key parts of quarterly and annual financial reports for the Deutsche Bank Group according to IFRS.
    *   Analyze and comment on the Group's key financial figures.
    *   Support the preparation of consolidated financial statements, notes, and the Group management report.
    *   Prepare key presentations on reporting topics.
*   **Stakeholder Management:**
    *   Manage communication and partnerships with internal and external stakeholders.
*   **Project Involvement:**
    *   Participate in finance organization projects.
    *   Support the development of reporting processes and tools.
*   **Continuous Improvement:**
    *   Actively contribute to process improvements in the finance area.
*   **Reporting Expertise:**
    *   Responsible for preparing important presentations on reporting topics.

**Your Profile**

*   **Education & Experience:**
    *   Completed university degree in economics with a focus on accounting, finance, or controlling.
    *   Several years of professional experience in group accounting, IFRS reporting, or auditing.
*   **Knowledge & Skills:**
    *   Sound knowledge of IFRS.
    *   Good understanding of group structures and processes.
    *   Presentation skills, analytical thinking, structured working method, and high level of self-initiative.
    *   Strong problem-solving skills and ability to be a team player.
    *   Excellent communication skills in English and German (oral and written).
*   **Ideal (Preferred) Experience:**
    *   Ideally experience in the professional leadership of employees or project teams.
*   **Personal Attributes:**
    *   Emotionally balanced and positive attitude.
    *   Strong work ethic and proactive approach.
    *   Team player with a strong network.
*   **Other:**
    *   Ability to work in both full-time and part-time roles.
    *   Openness to a diverse and inclusive work environment.
- **Validated Location**: Frankfurt

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## DWS - Business Functional Analyst (E-invoicing) - Requirements & Responsibilities

Here's a breakdown of the requirements and responsibilities:

**Your Tasks (Responsibilities)**

*   **Project Ownership:** Responsible for the efficient implementation of inbound and outbound e-invoicing processes, controls, and reporting.
*   **Process Definition & Setup:** Define, operate, and technically set up e-invoicing regulations in collaboration with various operational units, finance, tax, IT, and other stakeholders.
*   **Market Research:** Screen the German and European market for new e-invoicing transformation systems.
*   **System Adaptation:** Test and evaluate potential new software solutions. Design, coordinate, and conceptualize BRDs (Business Requirements Documents) for necessary adjustments to internal systems.
*   **Interface & Collaboration:** Act as a liaison between operations and IT subject matter experts. Collaborate closely with IT developers.
*   **Strategic Alignment:** Secure ongoing strategic approval from IT architecture and key decision-makers, aligning with DB's (Deutsche Bahn) strategic focus.
*   **Process Improvement:** Analyze, organize, digitize, and implement e-invoicing verification operations BAU (Business As Usual) process centralization.
*   **Automation:** Develop and implement automated oversight processes (KPIs, KRIs, MIS, dashboards, mail ticket tools).
*   **Documentation & Training:** Organize process documentation, training within the team with operational SMEs (Subject Matter Experts), and conduct internal audits.
*   **Business Continuity:** Define and document Business Continuity Plans.
*   **Compliance:** Ensure availability of all required attestations from Legal, Risk, Compliance, and Internal Audit.
*   **Communication:** Coordinate internal and external communication with DWS Coverage, Relationship Management, Product, German Vendors, and other stakeholders.
*   **Expansion:** Evaluate potential expansion of e-invoicing to EMEA (Europe, Middle East, and Africa) and other global DWS entities.
*   **Scalability:** Develop and implement a scalable and globally replicable process.
*   **Tax Reporting:** Collaborate with the company tax department, considering real-time tax reporting requirements.
*   **Automation & Integration:** Automate and implement automated booking & reconciliation processes as an interface between operations/finance/tax departments and tax authorities.
*   **Project Documentation:** Maintain project documentation.

**Your Profile (Requirements)**

*   **Education:** Successfully completed economic science studies, ideally with a focus on IT or equivalent training and professional experience.
*   **Experience:** Experience in operations, finance, and project management within asset management.
*   **Accounting Knowledge:** Bookkeeping knowledge, preferably in fund or financial accounting.
*   **System Proficiency:** Product and system knowledge (SimCorp Dimension/Aladdin/SAP).
*   **IT Understanding:** Development knowledge and experience in global IT interface and system integration projects.
*   **Software Skills:** Excellent knowledge of MS Office applications.
*   **Communication Skills:** Strong solution-oriented communication skills, very good German and English (written and spoken).
*   **Stakeholder Management:** Experience in dealing with internal and external customers and service providers in projects.
*   **Teamwork:** Willingness to help and teamwork skills.
*   **Learning Agility:** High willingness to learn and openness to new approaches.
*   **Collaboration:** Openness and ability to share information within the team, as well as to convey expertise and competence.
*   **Initiative:** High degree of initiative and well-considered, self-confident decision-making.
*   **Results-Oriented:** Solution-oriented willingness to improve the status quo and achieve measurable results.
*   **Growth Potential:** Potential for further development and a high sense of responsibility.
*   **Flexibility:** Willingness to work in a hybrid work model.
*   **Adaptability:** Willingness to accommodate adjustments to the application process, including interview formats and support in DW's facilities.
*   **Commitment:** A commitment to responsible action, business thinking, initiative, and goal-oriented collaboration.
- **Validated Location**: Frankfurt

*   **Design, implement, and maintain** Microsoft Power Automate Flows/Apps and RPA solutions to optimize HR business processes.

*   **Ensure system integrity and stability** within the Power Platform ecosystem, adhering to audit and compliance standards.
*   **Create comprehensive documentation** for developed apps and workflows to support maintainability and knowledge transfer.
*   **Streamline HR business processes** within an agile Scrum environment.
*   **Collaborate** closely with HR stakeholders and relevant COO units.
*   **Work with a variety of systems** including ServiceNow HRSD, AEM Forms, DocuSign, and Perceptive Content.

*   **Experience:** Several years of professional experience as a Flow Designer, ideally in an HR-related context.
*   **Technical Skills:**
    *   Proficient in tools like JIRA and Confluence.
    *   Experience with agile project management and collaboration in agile teams.
    *   Strong analytical, conceptual, and problem-solving skills.
    *   Familiarity with HR process optimization is a plus.
*   **Languages:** Very good German and English (written and spoken).

    *   Emotionally balanced and positive attitude.

    *   Ability to work independently and as part of a team.

    *   Openness to a full-time or part-time role.
    *   Willingness to participate in training and development opportunities.

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Sustainability Data Analyst - Requirements (English Translation)

Here's a breakdown of the requirements for the Sustainability Data Analyst position:

**Your Tasks:**

*   **Project Support:** Support international projects related to sustainability, working with the Chief Sustainability Office (CSO) and Technology & Data Innovation (TDI).
*   **Collaboration:** Work closely with the Sustainability Data and Technology Program lead, delivery teams, and stakeholders.
*   **Progress Monitoring:** Track project progress, identify and resolve roadblocks, and ensure plans are realistic.
*   **Financial & Resource Management:** Manage the financial, personnel, and investment aspects of the workstream.
*   **Risk & Issue Management:** Proactively manage risks, issues, and dependencies with other departments and initiatives.
*   **Cross-Functional Interaction:** Engage with various departments within the bank, from business to infrastructure, and interact with different levels of seniority.
*   **ESG Data & Technology:** Integrate technology, data, and innovation into sustainability-related data.
*   **Strategic Framework:** Support the development and coordination of the Bank's sustainability strategy and governance.
*   **Sustainable Finance:** Coordinate the planning of the Bank's Sustainable Finance targets.
*   **ESG Standards:** Assist in setting ESG standards.
*   **Regulatory Oversight:** Oversee regulatory and disclosure obligations.
*   **ESG Transparency:** Contribute to improving transparency regarding the Bank's sustainability agenda and performance.
*   **Materiality Assessment:** Support the development and implementation of Deutsche Bank‚Äôs approach to assessing the materiality of sustainability topics.
*   **ESG Rating Requests:** Coordinate responses to key ESG rating requests.
*   **Process Optimization:** Optimize and implement processes, ideally including controls.

**Your Profile:**

*   **Education:** Bachelor's degree with a Master's degree in Business and/or Technology.
*   **Project Management:** Strong project management experience, including managing international projects with multiple deliverables.
*   **Process Improvement:** Proven experience in optimizing and implementing processes, ideally including controls.
*   **Analytical Skills:** Ability to deliver quality results under pressure, combined with strong analytical, problem-solving skills and excellent conflict resolution skills.
*   **Time Management:** Ability to manage multiple tasks simultaneously, prioritize delivery, and negotiate effectively with stakeholders.
*   **ESG Interest:** Strong interest in ESG/sustainability, preferably with relevant work experience.
*   **Language Skills:** Fluent in both English and German.
*   **Personal Attributes:** Positive attitude, proactive, and collaborative.
*   **Values Alignment:** Commitment to responsible action, business acumen, initiative, and goal-oriented teamwork.
*   **Diversity & Inclusion:** Openness to and support of a positive, fair, and inclusive work environment.
- **Validated Location**: Frankfurt

**Professional Qualifications:**

*   Formal secretarial training or equivalent business education.

*   Ability to keep business and administrative processes running smoothly.

**Personal Qualities:**

*   You should enjoy challenging work and be able to stay calm under pressure.

*   You should be a quick learner and able to work independently and in a structured way.
*   You should be enthusiastic and proactive.
*   You should have strong communication and teamwork skills, and be focused on providing good service.

*   You should be proficient in using Microsoft Office (Word, Excel, PowerPoint), and ideally have experience with Deutsche Bank's internal systems (like DB Concur or dbBuyer).
*   You should have excellent German and English language skills, both written and spoken.

## üéØ ENHANCED REQUIREMENTS SECTION
- **Concise Description**: **Role Overview:** ## Requirements (Translated to English)

**Your Profile:**

*   **Education:** Master's or PhD degree in a quantitative field (e.g., Mathematical Finance, Statistics, Econometrics) or equivalent work experience.
*   **Experience:** Several years of experience in credit risk modeling (Probability of Default - PD, Loss Given Default - LGD, Capital Charge Factor - CCF).
*   **Knowledge:** Strong understanding of credit risk and relevant regulations (e.g., EU Capital Requirements Regulation (CRR), European Banking Authority guidelines on PD and LGD estimation).
*   **Skills:**
    *   Excellent analytical skills.
    *   Good statistical knowledge.
    *   Comfortable handling and optimization of large and complex datasets.
    *   Proficiency with statistical software (SAS) and programming skills in Python.
    *   Excellent communication skills in English (German is preferred).
*   **Personal Attributes:** Practical, results-oriented approach.

## Responsibilities

**Your Tasks:**

*   Development, implementation, and maintenance of industry-leading internal models (PD, LGD, CCF) for Deutsche Bank's credit portfolios.
*   Resolution of regulatory and internal findings related to credit risk parameter methodology or related models.
*   Close collaboration with various internal stakeholders (Business, Risk, Finance, Capital Management).
*   Presentation of models to regulators.
*   Ensuring models comply with regulatory requirements for credit risk parameter modeling.
*   Contributing to the Bank's efficiency, control, and transformation goals.
- **Validated Location**: Frankfurt
